Men's Basketball Semi-Finals

(I) Overcoming a Strong Enemy with Determination

Qingguang Lost 33 to 37

Amidst fervent enthusiasm, the match between Chizhi and Qingguang began. Qingguang started strong, but Chizhi resisted, winning the first half 15 to 14, a one-point lead. Although Qingguang briefly surpassed them in the second half, Chizhi, with their skilled and agile teamwork, ultimately overcame Qingguang 37 to 31. Cheers for their championship hopes rose even higher.

Qingguang Gains Momentum with a Two-Pronged Attack: Tan Dazhen scored the first point due to Qian Dingshen's foul. After some back and forth, Qingguang attacked from both sides, with Zhang Jinxiang of the left wing scoring a long shot. Xu Kepei also netted a backhand shot from a sharp angle. Qingguang scored five consecutive points, becoming unstoppable in just two minutes.

Chizhi Counters with a Point to Take the Lead: Seeing their unfavorable position, Chizhi called a timeout to discuss strategy. Sure enough, the five players worked seamlessly together, seizing every opportunity to advance and launch a major counterattack, scoring six consecutive goals. At this point, Qingguang also made substitutions, bringing in Lu Dazhen and Yu Quezi and changed their tactics, employing individual defensive strategies with tight marking. This effectively slowed Chizhi's momentum. Chizhi led 15 to 14 in the first half, winning by one point.

Qingguang's Revival is Fleeting: At the beginning of the second half, Qingguang suddenly showed signs of resurgence. Xu Kepei, Yu Quezi, and Zhang Jinxiang successively made contributions, quickly exceeding the score to 22 to 18. At the height of their momentum, Chizhi requested another timeout, breaking Qingguang's momentum. Chizhi then soared upwards, smoothly regaining control. Qingguang's revival was merely a flash in the pan.

Chizhi's Three Forwards are Unbelievably Skilled: Chizhi's victory was swift and decisive. Forwards Qian and Yang advanced like lightning, and with the ball in hand, they were already in front of the basket in the blink of an eye. Their agility and skill are rarely seen these days. Kong Guangyi's advances and retreats were composed and controlled, allowing him to attack and defend. Tan Dahua also performed exceptionally well, becoming increasingly brave and relentless as the game progressed. Qingguang was repeatedly broken through, allowing Chizhi to score eleven consecutive points, leading to a score of 29 to 22. Afterwards, the score difference remained between seven and eight points, and Qingguang was unable to recover. Qingguang's defeat was due to their inferior speed and agility compared to Chizhi, and their teamwork was not as skilled.

(II) Shanghai University Reaches the Peak

Jin'an Lost to Shanghai University 45 to 56. Following that, Jin'an and Shanghai University fought. For the first ten minutes, both sides were evenly matched. However, Jin'an suddenly took a two-point lead. Shanghai University then deployed its two great generals as guards, Lu and Wang, and defeated Jin'an by a wide margin. The level of interest was far below the previous match. Shanghai University gained the right to the finals. The score was 56 to 45.

Jin'an Takes a Two-Point Lead: Shanghai University launched a fierce attack from the start, with its three forwards dashing forward. Jin'an defended. Lu Puhui seized the opportunity to attack along the right side, scoring with one shot. Li Ruchun followed on the left. Shanghai University took an early lead of 4-0. Huang Zhaolin of Jin'an recovered three points, but Shanghai University extended the lead to 9-3. Jin'an then rested, reinforced, and changed its strategy. Wei Haiqing jumped for the ball and directly tapped it towards the basket. Huang Zhaolin caught up and scored three consecutive times, taking a two-point lead over Shanghai University, 13-11.

Shanghai University Reinforces with Two Great Generals: With this strategy in place, Jin'an's momentum increased. In an unfavorable position, Shanghai University urgently called on two great generals from the reserves to join the battle. Lu Zhongen and Wang Xiliang took up defensive positions in the back, guarding the rear, allowing the forwards to attack freely. After the score reached 15-19, Jin'an began an irreversible decline. Shanghai University won the first half 33 to 19.

The Three Unpredictable Generals: In the second half, Li Chengyuan of Jin'an was replaced by Cai Rongrui. Although Wei Haiqing managed to score one goal, the three young generals of Shanghai University, with their skillful and agile movements and swift footsteps, roamed unpredictably within Jin'an's territory and scored ten consecutive points. At this point, Shanghai University led by a great distance, 44-21.

Jin'an Loses Due to Poor Defense: Jin'an's defeat was already evident, and it was not easy to recover. Although Huang Zhaolin made a long shot that connected, the situation was terminal and ultimately ineffective. However, the score gradually became closer. Shanghai University won 56-45. Shanghai University's victory was certainly due to the reinforcement of the two guards and Qian Jingyong and Feng Nianhua's wonderful shooting skills, which were executed with ease and accuracy, a true marvel. Jin'an faced an extremely sharp offensive, but their defense was not strict enough; otherwise, they could have at least reduced Shanghai University's score. Moreover, inaccurate shooting was a major cause of Jin'an's failure.

Women's Basketball Bi-Weekly Tournament: Liangjiang's Great Victory Over Jin'an

Twenty-Two to Nine

As the series of sports competitions unfolded, the atmosphere grew increasingly tense. Yesterday's basketball game was scheduled to begin at 6 PM, but around 4 PM, many people were already standing outside the basketball court's entrance, waiting to buy tickets. When the final of the Wubu vs. Haixing match concluded on the track and field, even more people arrived, creating a massive crowd. By 5 PM, it was difficult to find a place to stand inside the basketball court. After 6 PM, countless people were unable to enter. While this situation created difficulties for the organizers, it was a positive sign for sports.

| Details of the Intense Battle |

First Quarter: Referee Zhou Jiaqi signaled the start of the game. The twelve ladies spread out across the court, each guarding their opponent, forming six pairs in pursuit of each other. Amidst applause, Ms. Yang Ren of Liangjiang scored first, opening the record. Ms. Liu Mali of Jin'an, tall and strong, ran back and forth tirelessly. Her skills were undoubtedly the best among the Jin'an players. Unfortunately, her teammates' skills as forwards were not as consistent, making it a difficult task for her to succeed alone. By the end of the first quarter, Liangjiang led 8-3.

Second Quarter: Jin'an's guards suddenly displayed courage and performed exceptionally well. Wang Lan's interceptions and steals were particularly praised by the audience. Although Liangjiang had renowned players like Shao Jingying, Yang Ren, and Long Jingxiong, who utilized the triangle passing formation, it was still difficult to score. They changed their strategy, passing the ball back to the rear to lure out Jin'an's defenders, and then attacking from the sidelines. They won the second quarter 5-2.

Third Quarter: The battle grew more intense, with the ball often staying in Jin'an's territory. The three guards of Jin'an defended against attacks, running almost continuously. However, they all fulfilled their duties, giving the forwards of Liangjiang few opportunities to shoot. At this time, the guards of Liangjiang supported the front line effectively. Wang Lan frequently made excellent moves, and Zhuang Shuyu maintained composure in motion, occasionally delivering surprises. Thus, after eight minutes of hard-fought struggle, Jin'an scored nothing, and Liangjiang only gained four points. This demonstrates the intensity of the competition at the time.

Fourth Quarter: Seeing the score of 17-5 on the scoreboard, the coach of Liangjiang knew that their victory was almost assured. Therefore, they substituted Long Jingxiong and Xiang Dawei with two new players, Song Wencheng and Chen Jiajun. As a result, the game became less exciting than before. However, Liangjiang still won the fourth quarter 5-4. The scorecards of the two teams are listed below:

Baseball Opening Game: Liyi Defeats St. John's

| Twelve to Seven |

Baseball is still in its infancy in Shanghai, so there are few talents. When the City Games were first being planned, there were concerns that no one would participate in the baseball competition. Unexpectedly, three teams registered, which was a pleasant surprise. Yesterday was the first act of the baseball games, featuring St. John's University against Liyi. In the end, St. John's lost to Liyi by a score of 7 to 12. The reporter knows that the readers must be wondering: Who exactly is Liyi organized by? Who are its team members? Before describing the details of the competition, I will give a brief introduction.

Introducing Liyi

The Liyi baseball team is organized by people who returned to Shanghai from Japan and are engaged in business. Among the team members is Zhang Jingpei, also known as Zhang Wen, who served as an outfielder for the Yokohama Chinese Athletic Association in Japan. He had a great reputation during his time in Japan. Wei Biao, also known as Wei Zongtang, who returned to Shanghai at the same time as Zhang, serves as a pitcher for the Chinese Athletic Association and has achieved good results. Li Wenxuan and Chen Guangrong also returned from the Yokohama Chinese Athletic Association and are now employed at the Yinxing Port and Yumao factories, respectively. In addition, Lin Wencheng, who used to be a pitcher for the Nanhua baseball team, is now also doing business in Shanghai and has joined Liyi. Therefore, Liyi is quite strong and has hopes of winning the championship. However, it seems that they lack practice. It is difficult to predict whether they can defeat Jiangwan (Fudan) today. We will have to explore the true situation during today's game.

Game Details

People in Shanghai have no interest in baseball games, so there were fewer spectators than team members. Compared to the volleyball game on the track and field, which was packed with people, and the basketball game in the basketball court, which was so crowded that there was no place to stand, it was truly frustrating.

Yesterday's game was divided into seven innings. The most exciting part was in the fourth inning when Liyi's pitcher hit a home run, instantly bringing back four runners. The score went from 5-4 to 9-4. Cheers erupted, with Japanese mixed with Cantonese, creating a loud wave of sound. This is because most of Liyi's team members are Guangdong overseas Chinese who were in Japan and later returned to China to do business. The other innings were not as exciting. They decided to select all the players for each item and each level on the same day, and then immediately begin the competition. A total of eight male athletes and one female athlete were selected. | Quiet Audience

Yesterday was the day of the repechage and finals. The audience was unusually excited. Before 2 PM, there were already no fewer than a thousand people standing around the stage. Then, because the volleyball game began, the number of people decreased slightly, but there were still many people watching, and they maintained order throughout.

| National Martial Arts Speech

Before the competition, Tong Zhongyi, the director of the Shaolin Department of the Municipal National Martial Arts Hall, gave a speech on stage about the significance of the National Martial Arts Competition, detailing which actions were legal and which were illegal during the competition in order to dispel the audience's misunderstandings. The audience applauded.

| Welcome Wrestling

The excitement of wrestling has been mentioned repeatedly in the newspapers, so the audience was particularly excited, and the repechage and finals were truly captivating. The first group in the repechage was Hong Zhifang against Song Baomao. Hong's agility was mentioned before. The opponent was also experienced, but his hooking skills were slightly inferior. Hong ultimately won 2-1. The next group was Liu Qinjun against Wang Sheng. Liu was physically strong, so Wang was not his opponent. However, Wang's wrestling skills were better, so he was able to hold on for a while. In the end, Liu still defeated Wang. The strengths and weaknesses of Liu and Hong Zhifang were similar, and Hong's wrestling skills were also better, but his strength was not as good as Liu's. He was ultimately held and knocked down twice. The power of a strong contender is truly awe-inspiring.

| For the True Swordsmanship

The first group in fencing was Lu Zishan against Shen Fulin, and the second group was Wang Xingsun against Xi Juncai. Both were able to use footwork and body techniques, but Shen and Xi each dropped their swords once, which was careless. During the finals, Lu Zishan and Wang Xingsun each used lively steps and were exceptionally agile. A spectator shouted, "This is true swordsmanship!"

| The Last Strike

There were only three groups in lightweight boxing yesterday, and only one group in light middleweight. No. 26 Zhu Qingyong was the most outstanding in lightweight. When he fought against his opponent, No. 1 Shu Shaozhe, in the finals, his fists were like raindrops, striking continuously. Shu was slightly smaller, but he was not weak either. After one defeat, the referee asked him if he wanted to compete again. He proudly replied, "Compete again!" However, his strength was ultimately inferior and he was defeated. After stepping down from the stage, he was mentally exhausted. The rescue team laid him on a stretcher, gave him medicine, and sent him home in an ambulance. Tan Yijia's striking technique in the light middleweight division was particularly outstanding. Although Liu Fengming was a martial arts expert who used both punches and kicks, he had to wait for opportunities to strike and did not score as many points as his opponent. Therefore, the boxing championship still belonged to Zhu Qingyong and Tan Yijia, thanks to their final efforts.

| Overall Review of the National Martial Arts Competition

This National Martial Arts Competition is unprecedented in China. It is natural that its achievements are not amazing. However, the winners of the championships, such as Liu Qinjun and Tan Yijia, cannot be said to be anything less than satisfactory. The women's championship, on the other hand, had few competitors and was won by one person. There was no opponent in the competition, so she was recommended by the organizing committee to participate in the National Games. Although her striking technique was obviously immature, it is hoped that the women's community will pay special attention to the equipment. The protective gear used was the modern military fencing gear, because there is no suitable protective gear for martial arts. It seems that this should be gradually studied in the future to avoid being ridiculed for using foreign goods. The reviewer of the boxing competition believes that it is neither Chinese nor Western, because it is designed for leather gloves. However, without leather gloves, the opponent will inevitably be injured. With gloves, the methods cannot be fully used. This is the biggest problem for future National Martial Arts Competitions. It is hoped that the authorities of the National Martial Arts Hall will conduct a thorough study.

| Prize Information

According to the organizing committee, the prizes will be awarded after the 20th. The location has been selected as the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. All winners of the National Martial Arts Championships will be notified by the organizing committee or the Municipal National Martial Arts Hall at that time. In addition, those who have excellent skills but did not win a championship will also be awarded prizes by the National Martial Arts Hall on a selected date as encouragement.

It is heard that the Municipal Staff Health Sports Competition, a new era of sports, is scheduled to be held on the 19th and 20th. The food supply has been prepared. Free Talk

Don't Remove the Weeds in the Courtyard, Anecdotes by a Vegetarian

The Professor of Florence

After Galileo discovered the four moons of Jupiter, he wrote an article that was published in the Starry Messenger Nuncius Siderius on January 24, 1610.

After this groundbreaking article was published, which would be so precious from today's perspective, the professors at the University of Florence looked down on it.

Faher wrote in his biography of Galileo that the chairman of philosophy at Padua did everything in his power to prevent the Grand Duke from believing in the existence of the four moons of Jupiter. He said:

"Animals have seven orifices on their heads, which allow air to circulate throughout their bodies, allowing them to see, stay warm, and grow. What are these seven orifices of this small universe? Two nostrils, two eyes, two ears, and one mouth. At the same time, in the grand universe of the heavens, there are two auspicious stars, two inauspicious stars, two luminous stars, and one transcendent, undecided Mercury. There are countless similarities of this kind, such as the seven metals being one example; therefore, we conclude that the number of planets must undoubtedly be seven. Furthermore, Jupiter's moons are not visible to the human eye, so they cannot have an effect on the earth, so they are useless, so they exist. Moreover, the Jews, ancient peoples, and modern Europeans have established seven days as a week and call them by the names of the seven planets. If we increase the number of planets, wouldn't we be overturning this beautiful system altogether?"

Galileo himself said:

"I would like to invite the professors of Florence to look at Jupiter's four satellites. They not only do not want to look at the stars, they do not even want to look at my telescope. They believe that there is no truth to be found in nature, truth is only in books."

How many of the Chinese professors are not from Florence? The native old scholars say: "Truth is only in ancient books." The foreign-returned scholars say: "Truth is only in foreign books." The lazy lecturers say: "Truth is only in the mouth." If young students believe these professors, they can be considered students naturalized in Florence. Who can build their own instruments to anchor themselves to nature? If there is such a person, I am willing to hold the broom and be his vegetarian.

World News in Brief

The European golf craze is now popular in Shanghai. Its origin is in big golf. According to research, golf existed on the European continent three hundred years ago. The Dutch painter Rembrandt's paintings include golf games. However, the clubs used by the people in the paintings are old-fashioned and somewhat different from modern ones. Golf is a game for the aristocracy because it takes up a lot of space. A small field is not enough to maneuver. Therefore, golf clubs in Europe and the United States charge a lot. Only the rich can afford it. However, recently, golf clubs in the UK have been considering reducing membership fees in view of the large number of people who love to play golf in order to popularize it. Small countries such as Yugoslavia are also popularizing golf. Their first golf course recently opened in Zagreb. General fans flock to it.

America's Crime Fever. The United States has many great industries. Recently, they have added another one, which is crime. According to a British weekly, there are as many as one million Americans who make a living by committing crimes. The annual number of cases includes 12,000 murders, 100,000 robberies, and 500,000 thefts. (Hai Ke)

A Tragic Report from a Page of Bandit Area

— Qifeng Louzhu

My friend Tang Jun serves in the 9th Division of the National Army. Last month, he was ordered to follow Commander Jiang to Gan County to suppress bandits. He traveled thousands of miles with great hardship. Now he has obtained a letter from him from Xingguo to Nanchang, which fully describes the situation in the disaster area. It is thousands of words long and makes people feel sad. The following are a few excerpts from the most important parts.

Tang wrote in his letter, "Of all the counties we passed through, Xingguo suffered the most severe disaster. When we first arrived (less than a week after we recaptured it), I think no one would want to come to this empty city. Now I will briefly describe the situation in this place. According to the investigation, this county had more than 20,000 residents before it was captured by bandits. Now, at most, there are less than 300 people left. Among them, women account for more than two-thirds. Most of the men are old and unable to work or have disabilities. Speaking of our supply problem, it is really difficult to the extreme. In addition to what we collect from the countryside, there are only firewood and rice. The most important oil and salt are simply impossible to purchase. Therefore, we have been eating plain rice for many days. Among them are the civilians who were captured by the bandits but did not escape. The price of the daily necessities they had previously stored (a very small amount) is really a strange story. I will also report it incidentally. Beautiful cigarettes cost two yuan per tin, salt costs one yuan per catty, foreign candles cost half a yuan per pack, white sugar costs one yuan per catty, and socks cost one yuan per pair. Kerosene costs fourteen yuan per tin. It can be said that it is extremely expensive. The market has long been empty. It is extremely miserable. The better houses have been destroyed by airplane bombs. There are still two pharmacies in the city, but the medicines are not fully stocked. There is one paper shop, selling only leftover goods. There are no other shops at all. Our team is stationed in the empty houses along the street. "Slightly omitted" Communist slogans are everywhere. Even the sides of the toilets and dung pits are covered with them. The most interesting one is "Oppose husbands beating their wives." Isn't that a joke? There are also "Down with the Cancellation Faction" and "Eliminate the AB Group" "......". This is the most obvious kind of internal division within the Communist Party. It is said that there were five or six thousand members of the AB Group of the Trotskyist faction in Xingguo County. Now the leader, Hu, has been killed by Peng Dehuai in Guangchang." Alas! Now the whole country is suffering from floods, and the people in the disaster areas are in a state of near death. How can we add to the banditry? The people are being tormented and oppressed. Our people have no one left to eat.

Picking Up Lingering Sounds from the Elegant Gathering at the Daya Building

— Mei

There is a silk and satin shop at the corner of Shilu and Sanmalu. It is called Daxin. It is intended to take the meaning of what the university calls "If you can renovate one day, renovate every day, keep renovating." The owner of the shop, Wang Yansong, took the 22nd of September as the one-week anniversary of the expansion of the business. In addition to instructing his subordinates to prepare for a grand anniversary sale, he also planned to publish a special issue for circulation. Therefore, he advertised for articles in early September, with the topic being "My Views on Saving the National Silk and Satin Industry." Another topic was "Hopes for the Daxin Silk and Satin Shop." He sincerely wanted to use the elegance of high-level articles to spread long-term strategies for salvation. His intentions were also bitter. The article submission deadline was the day before yesterday. The owner of the shop invited literary figures to hold a review meeting in the Daya Building. The meeting was not regular. It is important to record. So I will describe a few points to fill this talk.

The Reviewers Appointed Themselves as Chief Examiners. Those present that night included Pan Gongzhan, Hu Shuhua, Wang Xiaolai, Fang Jiaobo, Yan Duhhe, Zhou Qingjuan, Yan Esheng, Wang Xiaoying, and others. When Wang Xiaolai entered the door, he shouted, "The chief examiner is here." Then he said, "It is not easy to be a chief examiner. I am afraid I will be fined three months' salary." His words can be said to be humorous.

The Little Reporter Acts as a Pioneer. This review was conducted by each reviewer scoring individually, and then averaging the total score to determine the order of ranking. However, it is most difficult to start scoring each work first. The little reporter of the News Daily was pushed to be the pioneer and set the score first. Although the opinions of the chief examiners were different, the psychology of first impression was not without influence. As a result, the ranking after the overall review was not much different from the score set by the little reporter. The little reporter's effort was great.

Tang Naixin Was Highly Appreciated. There were seventy works submitted by women. Among them, the work of Tang Naiqi, a third-year student at the Shanghai Law School, was the best. It was thousands of words long and had many insights. The scores of the chief examiners were all above 96 points. Examiner Fang gave as many as 99 points. The public questioned him. He said, "Miss Tang is still studying and is studying law. Now she can eloquently describe the strategies for saving the national silk industry in such detail. How can we not give her extra points?" Miss Tang was so appreciated by the examiners. I can't help but congratulate Miss Tang on her future.

Thank You for Donating Your Royalties to Help the Disaster Victims. The royalties for the months of June and August from Tianxu Wosheng were 39 yuan and 88 cents. He Tianjian's royalty for August was 2 yuan. Zhang Shanzi's royalty for August was 9 cents. Da Zian's royalty for July was 1 yuan. Lan Qian's royalty for August was 72 cents. The total was 44 yuan and 50 cents. As instructed, it has been sent to Jin Cheng Bank for collection and used to relieve the disaster. The receipt is kept for verification. This is hereby disclosed. The editorial department of Free Talk thanks you on behalf of the disaster victims.

Random Notes from Fusang

— Ai Ai, Sent from Tokyo

The Magic of Coffee Waitresses

People who come to Japan for the first time must be very surprised. Why do the Japanese, especially young Japanese students, like to drink coffee so much? When we walk into a university area, the first thing we find are those small coffee shops with futurist patterns on their facades. This is just like Napoleon discovering some branches and aquatic plants before discovering the New World. It is a very interesting story.

According to a survey by the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department, as of March of this year, there are 3,215 coffee shops and 20,043 coffee waitresses in Tokyo alone. If we could statistically analyze the consumption of customers who enter and leave coffee shops every day, it would definitely be an astonishing number.

Because there are too many coffee shops, the business competition is very fierce. The owners of the coffee shops try their best to decorate them in a particularly novel way. Some decorate the seats in an antique style, as if they are holding an antique exhibition. Some are at the forefront of Europeanization. Recently, a coffee shop called Nichirin opened on Ginza, Japan's Broadway. The rainbow-like signs dazzle the eyes. However, the interior decoration is gloomy and remote like a forest. The dim green lights give off endless coolness. The enchanting songs of the waitresses are tempting passers-by. It is said that the income of Nichirin Coffee Shop on the first day of its opening was nearly 2,000 yuan. Who would believe that Japan is asking about the recession?

Many caring people often express worry and sigh about the romance of young people and the increase of these wine and woman hedonists. However, the government believes that it is better to let young people idle and study Marx and Nichols and do those things of meeting and forming associations. They are happy to turn a blind eye to this kind of entertainment.

The development of coffee shops is not accidental. On the one hand, young people need the comfort of the opposite sex, and these charming waitresses are delicate and considerate confidantes. On the other hand, women are eager to find a job, and of course the easiest job to make money is "coffee waitress." At the same time, their secondary purpose is to take the opportunity to find their ideal lover among the bustling customers. Therefore, in the past, those who became "coffee waitresses" were only graduates of senior elementary schools. Now, even female teachers and female college students have become "coffee waitresses." Japanese women have no so-called chastity in the waitress era. They think that selling smiles at this time is harmless. They have deeply forgotten their own pity and lightly forgive people's sins.

As the lights come on, those tens of thousands of waitresses are already ready. Their evening makeup, the raven-black temples, are adorned with sad and beautiful temple flowers. The delicate faces are thinly coated with rouge. Light makeup and heavy makeup, charming in every way. They are all working hard for money and paying attention to dressing up their own beauty. (This article is not finished)

Rotary Club of Storytelling

A Husband's Wife (16)

— Jiang Hongjiao

Mr. Li felt that he had to leave in front of Mr. Chen, so he left laughing. Mr. Chen sat on the sofa by the window, silently, watching her put on socks, put on clothes, wash her face, etc., which took another hour.

"Can we have dinner?" Mr. Chen was a little impatient. His stomach was really starving. He had eaten something at seven o'clock in the morning.

"You seem to have not eaten anything for three days. All day long, I only hear you complaining about hunger. I haven't had tea yet. How can I swallow the food?" She said, and then she was busy looking for tea leaves and jasmine flowers, and then she started the kerosene stove to boil water. It was not until 2:30 in the afternoon that she had lunch.

"Today is Sunday. Let's go to the movies!" She ordered like giving an imperial edict.

"I want to write a few letters."

"A man, hiding at home all day long, is really going to hide and get sick. If you don't go, I will go." She said, and then walked to the door and shouted, "Mr. Li! Let's go to the movies, okay?"

"Then you should also invite Mrs. Li to go together!" Mr. Chen interjected.

"She never goes. Why go and get a rebuff again?"

Mr. Li came dressed neatly in clothes and hats. He opened his mouth and said, "I have been waiting for you for a long time. Let's go! If we are late, we won't be able to get a good seat. Mr. Chen, why aren't you going?"

"He is really my good helper. He is willing to stay at home and take care of things. Let him be!" Mrs. Chen joked with a smile, while looking for clothes to change in the closet.

"You speak really interestingly! You are really a man. If I were a woman, I would really want to marry you as my wife." Mr. Chen also joked with a smile.

"Woman? A woman like you is really bad luck!" She was fastening her clothes buttons in front of the mirror, squinting at Mr. Chen and Mr. Li in the mirror.

"Why? Don't you think I am a very beautiful woman?" Mr. Chen stroked his Charlie Chaplin-style mustache.

"Are there any women in the world who have mustaches?" She said, and everyone laughed.

"Mr. Chen, change your clothes and come with us! Come with us!" Mr. Li urged, pulling on Mr. Chen's arm. He knew that Mr. Chen would not go, so he pretended to be diligent.

"I really have some things I want to finish while it's Sunday. You go. It's not early." Mr. Chen felt a little sourly stimulated in his heart, and he could not immediately explode.

Yesterday, the local securities market was very quiet, with only 6,000 yuan of 20th Year Customs Bonds traded. There were no other transactions. The forward market was also relatively calm, but trading activity was not entirely absent. Consolidated Tax, Salt Tax, and 20th Year Customs Bonds were actively traded. Volume totaled over 1,100,000 yuan in the morning and 5,700,000 yuan in the afternoon, for a combined total of over 15,800,000 yuan. The trend for the bond prices was generally calm, with no major fluctuations between the morning and afternoon sessions. However, due to active selling and quiet buying, prices gradually weakened. As a result, compared to the previous day, only the Reorganization bond price was stable, the 96 bond fluctuated minimally, and the 20th Year Customs Bond (spot) rose by 1.7 yuan compared to the previous week. The Consolidated Tax, Salt Tax, and other bonds fell by more than one yuan, with other bonds falling by small fractions ranging from 0.5 to 0.6 yuan. The bond market appears to have entered a period of consolidation.

Cotton Yarn Market Shows Slight Improvement

The yarn market has not undergone any major changes, but the trend is slightly firmer. This is because major players intend to cover their short positions this month. The near-month market is relatively strong, and the far-month market is also being pulled up. However, most people believe that the severe floods in various regions will inevitably lead to disappointment in the future. Therefore, they are unanimously selling short, while manufacturers are observing and waiting for changes before taking action.

Major Players Covering Short Positions in the Current Month: At the opening of the Renbiao market, the market sentiment was extremely weak, and the atmosphere softened. Prices for all months fell by 0.02 yuan, except for the far months, which rose by 0.02 yuan. In the afternoon, major players covered their short positions in the current month, leading to a firmer market tone. Additionally, the price of three-grade yarn rose, and prices for all months increased by 0.05 to 0.07 yuan. The total transaction volume was 17,650 bales. Buy orders included 1,100 bales for Gongtai, 1,250 bales for Tianlong, 600 bales for Gengfeng, 300 bales for Lichang, and 500 bales for Ruidah. Sell orders included 1,400 bales for Meiji, 700 bales for Deji, 550 bales for Gengfeng, and 450 bales for Changfeng. The closing prices are recorded below:

Yarn Sales are Not Bad: The sales of spot yarn are still good. According to statistics, various traders bought a total of 1,100 bales throughout the day. Traders within the industry bought 600 bales, and Han traders bought 800 bales of futures. The market is flat. Among the traders from other regions, Guangdong bought 185 bales, Han traders bought 155 bales, the inland region bought 75 bales, northern traders bought 50 bales, Tianjin bought 75 bales, Sichuan bought 160 bales, and miscellaneous traders bought 100 bales.

Cotton Market Weakens

Rumor of the US Lending a Large Amount of American Cotton to China

The cotton market is showing signs of weakness. This is due to the decline in imported cotton prices and the rumor that the US government will lend 600,000 bales of American cotton to China on credit. This rumor is increasing the pressure from all sides, and many are selling off their holdings. However, Han traders are actively buying because of the severe floods in their regions, which have caused significant damage and made it impossible for them to deliver goods to Shanghai. The general situation is pessimistic, and the future is uncertain.

Han Traders Compete to Sell: At the opening of the Hanbiao market, the market conditions were very weak. Because American cotton had fallen again, major players sold off their holdings at the closing, due to the rumor that American cotton would be lent to China on credit. Prices for all months fell by 0.01 to 0.02 yuan. The afternoon was flat, and the gold market stabilized. Prices for all months rose by 0.005 yuan. The total transaction volume was 61,800 dan. Sell orders included 5,400 dan for Changhe, 5,300 dan for Xincheng, 2,500 dan for Yuda, and 5,400 dan for Dachang. Buy orders included 3,900 dan for Houfeng, 2,700 dan for Shenchang, 2,400 dan for Ruidah, and 2,500 dan for Xinfeng. The closing prices are recorded below:

Foreign Yarn and Cotton Decline Again

American Cotton: South Selling Short. Yesterday, American cotton was initially firm due to positive news from Liverpool, but weakened due to selling from the South and favorable weather. Futures fell by 13 to 16 points, and spot fell by 10 points. British cotton futures fell by 1 to 2 points, and spot rose by 9 points. Egyptian cotton spot rose by 25 points. Indian cotton was slightly bought by Japanese traders and brokers. The market was calm and stable. The price of Pingguoer rose by 0.75 rupees, Omla rose by 1 rupee, and Bairoxi rose by 1.25 rupees. Grain: River Rice Market Sales Stagnant, Prices Weak

South Market: Yesterday, there was a slight influx of goods from various regions. Although the weather was damp and overcast, retail sales in urban and rural areas were sluggish due to the approaching Mid-Autumn Festival and the lower prices in the northern market. Transactions decreased significantly. Sales were sluggish due to unfavorable weather, and prices had to be slightly lowered. The prices of thick japonica rice were not high, only recovering a small amount. Lower-grade rice had accumulated, and there was still sluggish demand for glutinous rice. This market is only interested in fresh rice. Central rice was completely stagnant. The market price was clearly fixed but secretly weakening. Given the overcast weather, the entry of new rice was hindered, and no major changes are expected. Demand for new japonica rice is declining, and the market continues to weaken. Yesterday, new Yangjian and new Dujian rice arrived from Xitang (approximately 180 shi) and Pingwang (approximately 160 shi). The quality of the rice was good. New Chuanjian rice from Jiaoli arrived (approximately 8 shi) and was of good quality, with a price of 15.3 yuan. New Xiangjing rice also arrived from Jiaoli (approximately 30 shi), with beautiful quality and a price of 18 yuan.

New Zha Market: Yesterday, the supply of Northern Jiangsu rice from Changshu and Wuxi continued to flood in, and there was a slight stock in the river. Retail demand was scarce due to the change in weather to sunny, and people were bearish. The prices of thick japonica, early glutinous, and thin glutinous rice all fell by 0.1 to 0.2 yuan. The prices of new japonica and new Yangjian rice fell by 0.2 to 0.3 yuan. Although there were few old Yangjian, Dujian, and Bujian rice, the demand was low, and there were no significant changes in price. Modified and deteriorated rice continued to decline and sales were normal. The market was uneventful. Spot sales of foreign rice were slightly active, and the market trended towards consolidation.

Large-Scale Sales of Future Foreign Rice

Yesterday, the foreign long-grain rice market was sluggish due to slightly weaker demand in this market. Foreign firms released a large number of future orders, and the market immediately reacted negatively. Both futures and spot prices weakened by a small amount. 210 bags of Jiangxi machine rice were released at a price of 14.2 yuan. 600 bags of Taizhou white rice were released at a price of 12.75 yuan to 12.3 yuan. 300 bags of Mindang rice were released at a price of 13.25 yuan to 13.2 yuan. 1,000 bags of Xiaojiao were released at a price of 13.05 yuan. Trading of future rice was very active yesterday, with all sales coming from foreign firms. 600 tons of Saigon No. 1 rice were sold at a price of 6.7 mace by Yuanli. Sassoon sold another 300 tons of October rice at a price of 6.71 mace. Mitsui sold 500 tons of Xiaojiao for October delivery, and Yuanfeng sold another 900 tons, both at a price of 6.15 mace.

Flour Futures Continue to Decline

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the market for various months showed a sluggish and continued downward trend. Although the quoted price of foreign wheat recovered by about 0.2 yuan, the nature of the huge amount of chips in the market, and the fact that most of them belonged to non-industry players, was not taken into account. They were simply speculative ventures. More recently, with the agreement for a large shipment of foreign wheat for disaster relief, the poor sales prospects for flour were apparent. Therefore, after the despair of the bulls, they had no choice but to gradually sell in reverse to seek a settlement. If these buyers were actual sales traders, they could perhaps be restrained or collected upon maturity, and would not be so panicked, placing themselves in such a desperate situation. Looking ahead, if there are further transactions of Russian wheat, the market shock may need to be further intensified. As a result, September and October fell by 0.075 yuan compared to the previous day, November and December fell by 0.01 yuan, and January and February fell by 0.075 yuan.

Wheat Futures: Heavily Burdened, Difficult to Reverse

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, the market for various months continued to decline. The market situation seemed to be heavily burdened and difficult to reverse, with an inevitable downward trend. It was also rumored that a foreign firm had already received a ship of foreign wheat and would soon receive more. Since no one was interested in buying it from the factories, they entrusted brokers to sell it off in the market. This type of seller was actually delivering real goods, which made people even more nervous and dealt a heavy blow. Given that the market trend is that supply exceeds demand and the factories are standing by, the collapse in the future may be inevitable. As a result, the current month fell by 0.02 yuan compared to the previous day, October, November, and December each fell by 0.04 yuan, and January and February each fell by 0.05 yuan. The spot wheat market has been quiet for a long time. Yesterday, 16,000 to 17,000 bags were opened, which were sellers drawing and selling to prepare for delivery. Wheat from Yangzhou and Zhenjiang was priced as high as 3.6 taels, and the second grade was 3.55 taels. Wheat from Gaoyou was 3.48 taels. Shenda handled 10,000 bags, and Huafeng handled more than 6,000 bags.

Sugar Market: Taikoo Sugar Gradually Showing Signs of Shortage

Yesterday, the sugar market production area telegram stated that the price of Cuban spot sugar had not changed. The price of New York sugar futures fell by 0.01 to 0.03 yuan in the near term, while the 500-share far term rose by 0.03 yuan. The price of Javanese spot and futures sugar also remained unchanged. The guild allocated 24th grade coarse white sand sugar Dutch sugar, but buying interest was sluggish, and the number of sellers was surging. The asking price for new goods was 11.6 taels, and the asking price for new 20th grade medium white sand sugar was 11.1 taels, but few were accepted. The asking price for 16th grade medium white sand sugar was 10.09 taels, and there were some transactions, but the market was not remarkable. The sales of Taikoo Sugar in various places were slightly smoother, and the stock in the market was very thin, especially for mid-range goods, which showed the greatest signs of shortage. B mark was 11.05 taels, old goods were 12 taels. DY mark was 11.95 taels. The number of sellers was declining, and some were asking 12 taels for the future. HM mark was 11.475 taels, and the market was also tight, trending gradually. The factory prices were particularly tight, and the fixed prices for each were: B mark 5.05 yuan, CW mark 5.00 yuan, DY mark 4.95 yuan, HX mark 4.90 yuan, HM mark 4.70 yuan, and H mark 4.60 yuan, with no room for negotiation. Although the traders intended to buy, the allocated prices were too high, resulting in them being helpless and sighing at the ocean, which is a separate view amidst the boycott of inferior goods.

Zhabei Goods: Newly Arrived Bozhou Peaches Sold Quickly

The first batch of new Bozhou peaches arrived the day before yesterday, totaling 67 bags. The peaches were very dry and of good size. They were all purchased by Ningbo, Shanghai, and other traders, and the price was 18.5 taels. Yesterday, the second batch of 40 bags arrived, and the quality of the goods was similar to the previous batch. Given the current need for various traders, the trend is very firm, and a further price increase may be necessary.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Silk Firms: Silk

Flourishing Trade in Gongxi Green Tea

Yesterday, in the tea market of foreign firms in this port, there was no lack of effort from the Russian Assistance Society in searching and purchasing Gongxi green tea from Wuyuan, Tunxi, and other routes. The newly established Yulong Foreign Firm also purchased a lot. The total transaction volume for the city was over 1,200 boxes, and the trade was quite prosperous. Firms like Xiehe, Tongfu, Doud, and Yongxing were also actively replenishing their stocks of Zhenmei pearl tea and other varieties, making the market more active. Chinese merchants, seeing their inventories dwindling, were unwilling to lower prices to sell the tea they held. The future of green tea is said to be very stable.

Checked Flannel Blankets Completely Searched Out

Flannel is usually sold in summer. With the arrival of autumn coolness, various heavy overcoat wool fabrics have been successively launched. Flannel should have been on the decline. Unexpectedly, checked flannel has recently become popular in the market, and the selling price has suddenly risen. Upon investigation, hat makers in this street have been searching for it to make small hats. At the same time, merchants from Sichuan have also started purchasing it, leading to a sudden tightening of the trend. However, the total stock in the city is limited. In the past three days, it has been completely searched out. It is quite unexpected that goods that should be declining would have such activity.

Dalian Ironmongers Urgently Procuring Black Sheet Metal

The hardware trade remains slack. Apart from a few scattered transactions, there are very few large-scale deals in the city. However, the Dalian ironmongers have emerged as a force to be reckoned with, urgently procuring black sheet metal. Therefore, it is quite gratifying for the whole city. It has been found that firms like Yilong, Chengyi, Chengyong, Ririsheng, and Hengzhu have collectively purchased as many as 2,250 bundles. As for the price, 18 sheets per load are estimated at 11 taels each, 36-inch sheets from 3 to 8 sheets are estimated at 9 taels and 4.5 qian, 9 to 10 sheets at 9 taels and 7.5 qian, 11 to 12 sheets at 10 taels and 0.25 qian, and 13 sheets at 11 taels and 5 qian. It has been found that the 18-sheet variety is the most purchased. However, the inventory of this product is extremely low, so there is hope for a continued rise in the market standard in the future.

Page 13

Local News

The Municipal Supervisory Committee Pays Attention to the Lives of Disaster Victims

Investigating Separately for Days

Proposes Five Points for Improvement

The Municipal Party Department Supervisory Committee, in light of the widespread floods and the increasing number of refugees arriving in Shanghai, even though the government has been trying to accommodate them, believes that their living conditions are worthy of attention. It dispatched personnel to various shelters for several days to conduct detailed investigations. Based on observations, it proposed five points for improvement, which were passed by the fifth Supervisory Committee meeting the day before yesterday and sent to the Executive Committee to be forwarded to the Social Bureau for implementation. The content is roughly as follows: "The shelters at Chaohui Villa, Quzhenren Temple, and Yongxitang on Xietu Road are temporary in nature, and it is difficult to ensure complete facilities. It is understood that the construction project of the disaster victim shelter on Liuying Road in Zhabei is nearing completion. Once the arrangements are complete, the disaster victims in the temporary shelters on Xietu Road will all be moved to Zhabei to be gathered in one place, which will be better for management and hygiene. However, based on past observations, the disorder and confusion are significant, and there is no order. Regarding the areas that need improvement, the five most important points are listed below:

The Supply of Provisions Should Be Uniform: The disaster victims come from Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui provinces, and Gaobao County in Jiangsu. There are differences in when they arrive in Shanghai, and the supply of provisions varies from time to time. Sometimes cash is issued, sometimes raw rice, or bread, biscuits, steamed buns, etc., are issued. Sometimes it is issued daily, sometimes every few days, sometimes several times a day, or only part of it is issued and not everyone receives it. The methods are very inconsistent. Whenever group representatives or newspaper reporters come to inquire, the disaster victims often complain about their hardships, hunger, and unfair treatment. Those who listen and do not understand are most likely to cause misunderstandings. In the future, it is best to calculate and distribute food according to the number of people, providing two meals a day, so that the weak are not harmed. If charitable organizations provide aid, it should also be collected and distributed uniformly by the Social Bureau to avoid disputes.

Registration Must Be Accurate: The number of disaster victims is large, and they live scattered everywhere, both inside and outside the gates. It is not possible to prohibit them from entering and exiting at will. It is difficult to get an accurate count by checking around the room. Even when asking the staff, they only give rough estimates. Some cunning disaster victims, when their requests are not met, attack the staff when group representatives or philanthropists come to inquire about the situation, claiming that they are inflating the numbers and enriching themselves at public expense. If false information is spread and published in newspapers, it will have a significant impact on the future of disaster relief. In the future, it is best to stipulate that several people live in one room, instead of scattering them outdoors. The bedrooms should be numbered in order, and the names of the disaster victims living in each room should be pasted outside the window, so that it is known how many people are in each room. By calculating in order, the total number can be obtained. The disaster victims will have no loopholes to exploit, and rumors will naturally cease.

Management Should Be Strict: The disaster victims come from other places, and since there are so many people, it is inevitable that they will be of mixed quality. Whenever charitable organizations send food for distribution, they gather in a corner, scrambling and fighting for it, shouting and making noise, making it difficult to describe. The strong push their way to the front to grab more, while the weak are unable to squeeze through and can only sigh as they watch. As a result, the full become fuller, and the hungry become hungrier, which completely loses the meaning of fairness and should be improved. In the future, when aid is delivered, it should be entrusted to the staff of the Social Bureau, who will determine the quantity and, together with the police stationed there, supervise the workers to distribute it in order of the bedrooms, so as to avoid the malpractice of scrambling and unfairness.

Pay Attention to Public Hygiene: The disaster victims come from the countryside, and most are farmers and workers with little knowledge. Children often urinate and defecate at will in the corners of the houses and in front of the courtyards. Once it is rained on and exposed to the sun, the foul odor spreads everywhere, which is extremely harmful to hygiene. It is appropriate to designate locations and have them comply. If someone is lazy and does not move forward, the police stationed there should intervene at any time. In addition, clothing should be washed frequently, and dust and dirt inside and outside the rooms should be swept away at any time, especially leftover food.

Find a Way to Provide Tea and Water: In the vicinity of the temporary shelters on Xietu Road, there are no boilers providing boiled water, and the shelters have not prepared any in advance. Some people quench their thirst with raw water. Those who survive disasters are most likely to get sick. Now that they have been moved to Zhabei, it seems appropriate to find a way to prepare a large amount of boiled water for their needs.

The above five points are only those that are simple and easy to implement. If they can be put into practice, the disaster victims will benefit immensely. However, the disaster is huge and funds are short, and the future is long. The disaster relief funds should also be allocated daily by the Emergency Relief Association, or a special fund should be designated by the government, which would be more appropriate.

Disaster Relief News from Various Provinces Yesterday

News from the National Government Disaster Relief Committee

Zhu Qinglan's Opinion: Zhu Qinglan, Standing Committee Member of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, expressed his opinion on the matter of allocating relief funds yesterday, saying that all relief funds donated by various sectors must be completely given to the disaster victims. All expenses, as well as any funds needed for any matters related to disaster relief, should, in my opinion, be borne by the government. I mentioned this matter to Chairman Song last time, and Song also expressed strong agreement. Therefore, all funds allocated to the disaster areas should be done in this way.

Japanese Representatives Arrive in Shanghai: In addition to donating a large quantity of relief supplies worth 300,000 Japanese yen, various sectors in Japan have also sent Mr. Fukao as a disaster relief representative, who arrived in Shanghai on the Nagasaki Maru at around 3:00 p.m. yesterday. Zhu Qinglan, Standing Committee Member of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, and Guo Dehua, a representative of the Propaganda Division, went to the Huishan Wharf to welcome Mr. Fukao, who is scheduled to go to the disaster areas along the Yangtze River tomorrow with Mr. Funatsu, a representative from Shanghai, to express their condolences.

Distribution of Relief Funds in Jiangsu: The 300,000 yuan in relief funds previously allocated to Jiangsu Province by the National Government Disaster Relief Committee has now been allocated as follows: Jiangdu 30,000, Gaoyou 30,000, Xinghua 40,000, Taixian 30,000, Jiangpu 5,000, Baoying 30,000, Dongtai 30,000, Yancheng 30,000, Liuhe 5,000, Liyang 4,000, Yixing 5,000, Lishui 3,000, Wanchun 3,000, Wujiang 5,000, totaling 250,000. The remaining 50,000 will be given to the shelters. In addition, the Relief Association plans to set up 22 shelters: Jiangdu 3, Gaoyou 2, Taixian 5, Baoying 2, Dongtai 2, Zhenjiang 3, Rugao 1, Tongxian 2, Jieshou 1, Sishui 1. In addition, it is planned to continue to allocate 35,000 yuan worth of No. 3 flour, which will be sent by Miao Jing Xinfen Flour Factory.

Joint Meeting of Relief Organizations Yesterday

The Shanghai Fundraising Emergency Relief Association for Flood Disasters in Various Provinces convened a meeting yesterday of various flood disaster relief organizations in Shanghai at Renji Hall to jointly discuss ways to coordinate. The representatives from various organizations who attended included Qu Yingguang, Wang Xiaolai, Li Zutan, and Wu Zhihao from the Emergency Relief Association, Wang Yiting from the Qing Sheng Association, Zhu Yinjiang from the Chinese and Foreign Joint Relief Association, Li Hanyin and Luo Dingchen from the Swastika Society, Lu Wenzhong from the Lianyi Charity Association, Liu Zigu from the Hubei Emergency Relief Association's Shanghai Office, Xu Jiyu from the Wuhu Charity Relief Association, Ren Jinping from the Ning Shao Relief Association for the Hankou Disaster, Xu Shao Liu from the Jiangsu Charity Relief Association, Li Lishu, Director of the Huai Huai Si Investigation and Relief, Ye Kaixin from the Hunan Fundraising Shanghai Office, and Yuan Ying from the Chinese Buddhist Association, among others, totaling more than ten people. Qu Yingguang was elected as chairman. First, Li Zutan gave a report, saying that the scope of this flood disaster is vast and the number of disaster victims is large, which is unprecedented. Various charitable organizations in Shanghai, based on the spirit of human mutual assistance and the compassion for the hungry and drowning, have risen up to raise donations with great enthusiasm. However, in order to understand the relief situation clearly and to promote mutual assistance and cooperation, it is necessary to connect with each other. This is the main purpose of today's meeting. Then, each representative expressed their opinions separately, and they all agreed that the mutual assistance and connection between the organizations is beneficial to the progress of disaster relief. Finally, it was decided to organize a joint meeting of Shanghai flood disaster relief organizations, and Li Zuyu was publicly elected to draft the meeting's charter. The organizations that attended the meeting jointly initiated the meeting and decided to reconvene next week to discuss the charter. The meeting adjourned at around 5:00 p.m.

Current Situation of Municipal Shelters

Since the completion of the first shelter in Zhabei, the situation at the Shanghai Shelter for Disaster Victims Office has gradually become more organized as disaster victims are concentrated in the shelters. However, the number of disaster victims arriving in Shanghai every day is very large. The Jinghu train arrived at the North Station the night before last, carrying about 500 refugees from the Jiangbei area. The office sent personnel to take care of them at the station and transport them to the shelters. However, at least half of these 500 people were not genuine flood disaster victims. Some were workers working in various factories in Shanghai, some were currently in their hometowns, and some were poor people who came to Shanghai to look for relatives and friends to make a living. All took this opportunity to mix with the disaster victims and take a free train to Shanghai, so it was not convenient to accommodate them all. However, it would not be appropriate to let them stay outside, in case they did not find their relatives and had nowhere to stay, turning them into refugees as well. The Fourth Office Affairs Meeting discussed this matter and decided to temporarily set up a temporary shelter in Zhabei. If any disaster victims arriving in Shanghai needed to find relatives and friends, the shelter would help them find and hand them over, so as to avoid them becoming vagrant. Those who had no relatives to turn to would be sent to the first shelter. In addition, many other important cases were discussed.

Fundraising for Clothing and Food: The shelter staff meeting decided that (1) regarding the disaster victims' clothing, it was decided to make 3,000 sets of single-layer clothing (it has been found that 1,000 sets have been made, and only 2,000 sets need to be made), costing more than 8 jiao per set, requiring about 3,000 yuan, and 3,000 sets of cotton clothing, costing 2.5 yuan per set, requiring about 7,500 yuan. One thousand five hundred quilts will be made first, costing about 5,000 to 6,000 yuan. In cold weather, straw mats will be laid on the lower bunks, with a single quilt on top, requiring a total of about 19,000 yuan. (2) Regarding the disaster victims' food, it was decided to purchase 100 shi of relatively coarse japonica rice and 500 bags of small ground rice. Japonica rice will be used to cook porridge, and small ground rice will be used to cook rice. Vegetables will be purely vegetarian, with vegetable oil added to make them delicious. (3) The office, noting that the disaster victims' children were malnourished, with yellow faces and weak bodies, decided to add soy milk, biscuits, and other foods every day to supplement their nutrition, which will be handled at the discretion of the hygiene team.

Financial Report: Feng Liutang, Director of General Affairs, reported on the financial situation, saying that on the income side, the municipal government allocated 50,000 yuan to the office, which has been fully received in installments, and donations from various sectors totaled 6,874 yuan, for a total of 56,874 yuan. On the expenditure side, the cost of provisions was 3,488 yuan 3 jiao 2 fen (in addition, the cost of food issued by the Tongren Fuyuan Hall was not included in the calculation), the construction cost of the first shelter was 3,293 yuan 3 jiao 6 fen (the total cost of the first shelter was 25,600 yuan, and only one batch has been allocated), and the emergency relief funds for the Yin Xing flood disaster was 1,300 yuan (this fund was approved by the Social Bureau to be allocated to the municipal commissioners of Yin Xing District for collection, and the Social Bureau has been replied to instructing the commissioners to prepare a roster of disaster victims so that they can be distributed to each household together), the clothing cost was 861 yuan 9 jiao, and the staff transportation cost was 284 yuan 7 jiao 4 fen (including 193 yuan for the food expenses of the police brigade). The remaining hygiene expenses were 392 yuan 2 jiao 9 fen, and the lecture and placement expenses were more than 1,500 yuan, for a total expenditure of more than 11,200 yuan. After offsetting income and expenses, there was still a surplus of more than 45,000 yuan, which was all deposited in the Shanghai Municipal Bank.

The Tragedy of Xinzhou: The disaster situation in Yongzhen Township, Yangzhou has been disclosed in newspapers. Now I have received a letter from Wang Mianzhi, a disaster victim in Xinzhou, (the above is omitted) Our place is in a flood waiting for rescue. I would like to present it to the elders. Please pray for pity and save it. On July 13, the early tide suddenly rose by four or five feet, and the wind and waves collapsed more than 50 houses in the Yongji Island and Tiancheng Island areas. All food, clothing, and belongings such as chickens and dogs were floating in the air. An old woman surnamed He and three children surnamed Chen drowned. At the same time, the western Jiang Tankou, Zhongxing Town Dawei and the eight people, Santang, Doubao, Jishan, Sixteen, and other ten or so weirs were broken and the sound of crying shook the sky. Fortunately, the evening tide was not large. Except for the Xijiang embankment and the two places in Bamin, there was no mud to block them. Autumn harvest is completely hopeless, hundreds of disaster victims are in the water every day, three or four feet deep and two or three feet shallow. All kinds of poisonous snakes, centipedes, come and go in the home, and live with people, waiting to be fed, with no food or clothing. Although we ask for help from all over, they are all neglected because the disaster area is small. Isn't it terrible? However, the disaster victims in Bizhou Weir have rice to salvage, and the disaster victims in Yongji Tiancheng and upland dry valleys are the hardest. Those with a little energy temporarily move to other places. Now there are more than 20 families left, including Mianzhi, who have no way to escape death. All the old and young people have no choice but to elect Mianzhi as their representative and go to Shanghai to plead with the folks and the great philanthropists of the time to give alms and save the dying and living dead fish. Gong Mo is also very big. (The following is omitted)

The Disaster Situation in Dangshan: Guo Jixin, chief of the Yangshan Farmers Association, sent a document as follows. The disaster situation is very serious, and the people cannot live. I hope that the council will grant relief funds to relieve the people and secure the local area. Because Dangyi has a poor geological quality, and is known as barren, in the old Xushu counties, it is known as the most bitter year-round soldiers and bandits, and famine is recommended. It has long been empty, and all opportunities for life have been exhausted. In the past few years, disasters have been reported one after another. Fortunately, at that time, various charities gave generously, allocated funds for relief, and saved countless lives. However, in the late summer and autumn of this year, the torrential rains lasted for more than two months, and the flood flooded the plain, four or five feet deep in some places and two or three feet shallow in others. In addition, Dangyi is humble, and the water in eastern Henan flows into the border, causing six or seven of the counties to become swamps. Early autumn harvest is only one or two, and late autumn is almost without seeds. What is the crime of the Dang people? I suffered this disaster. At the beginning of autumn, food prices skyrocketed. It is extremely difficult to buy food in towns and villages. It is true that the wheat harvest this year is not abundant, and even well-to-do families have no surplus grain. The poorest and poorest families buy grain to eat. Based on the harvest of wheat this year and the number of people in the county, if it is winter and spring, one-tenth of those who can eat again every day, two-tenths of those who can eat one meal, three-tenths of those who eat every other day, and the others who are displaced begging and waiting to die will be four or five-tenths. Quji will arrive next year in the wheat autumn, when there will be more than 300 days. If there is no relief policy, few orphans will be left. What is even more painful is that in the year of abundance, Dang people have meager income due to barren land, and by the time they are on holiday, they will have to support the old and carry the young and beg for food in Guanggu, Henan, Ying, Hao, Hao, Si, and other places in Anhui in order to survive. This year, all the above places have become disaster areas, and the Dang people have no place to find food and no way to live. If relief is not provided early, the weak will fill the trenches, the strong will take risks, and the future will be difficult to imagine. The association thinks about the situation, is heartbroken, and intends to ask Junhui to quickly allocate a huge amount of money to set up relief to save the people and secure the local area. I am very grateful and await orders. Presented to the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association,

Anhui Relief Association Sends Personnel to Shanghai to Appeal

Qiu Yuanwu, Standing Committee Member of the Anhui Provincial Relief Committee, came to Shanghai from Beijing the day before yesterday to appeal for the disaster situation in the province. Yesterday (17th), he met with Xu Shiying and Guan Jianfan, members of the Anhui Nationality of the Central Relief Committee and the National Flood Relief Association, and attended the Anhui Shanghai Fellow Flood Relief Tea Party to report on the actual situation of the floods in the province and jointly discuss relief methods. It is said that this time, 48 counties in Anhui were affected by the disaster, and the actual situation was even worse than that in Hubei and Jiangsu. However, due to lack of appeal, the outside world knows little about it. To this day, counties along the Yangtze River and the Huai River are still submerged in water. The entire county of Wuhe is submerged. There are floating corpses on the Jianghuai Water. There are still hundreds of corpses piled up on the mountains on the east and west sides of Liangshan, and they are allowed to rot and float. It is unbearable to see. According to reports, more than 8,000 people were drowned in Huoqiu County, including those with confirmed names. The collapse of Guangfeng Weir and the economic lifeline of Huaining counties have bankrupted tens of thousands of disaster victims, and they have gathered in the suburbs of the provincial capital. The weirs and fields in the entire province have been completely wiped out. The rest of the counties in Huizhou, although some have mountain fields, have also been washed away by mountain floods. The wheat season in northern Anhui has already been harvested, but it has also been washed away. In total, the disaster area in the province accounts for five-sixths of the entire territory, the disaster victims account for seven-eighths of the total number of people, and hundreds of thousands of people and animals have been drowned. The source of food production in the entire province has been cut off, and the disaster victims are crying for food day and night. A few days ago, disaster victims in various places along the Yangtze River were still climbing on the tops of houses and trees, desperately calling for help, but those who could not be rescued have been gradually starving to death and drifting away with the flow. It is heard every day that the existing disaster victims are waiting for rescue, and as a result, they are starving to death or throwing themselves into the water. The central government's emergency relief of 170,000 yuan has only been allocated to the ten counties with the most severe disasters, and it has not been able to reach them. In summary, it is also a drop in the bucket. At present, the disaster victims in the entire province can only wait to die. If there is no relief, the future will be terrible. It is also said that in the past, some charitable organizations or individuals generously donated relief, and most of them directly sent personnel or entrusted local individuals to handle the distribution, which caused great malpractices. The disaster victims hardly got any real benefits. First, there was no overall planning, and it was difficult to ensure that it was not biased and uneven. Second, they were full of food and drink. In the future, if there are fundraising relief funds in other places, it is best to entrust the provincial relief committee to take overall consideration and be responsible for it.

The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors Decides on Interest Rate Guarantee Measures

Funds Cannot Be Borrowed Without Completing the Procedures

Continued Meeting Scheduled for November 4th

The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors held meetings at the Bankers' Association for two consecutive days, which concluded the day before yesterday. According to a certain Chinese director who stayed in Shanghai speaking to this newspaper's reporter yesterday, the British refund of the Boxer Indemnity, including accumulated portions, is approximately 2.8 million gold pounds, all of which have been transferred to the London Purchasing Committee for safekeeping. According to the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Exchange of Notes, half is used for purchasing materials in England and half is used domestically. Two-thirds goes to the Ministry of Railways, and one-third is divided as follows: 40% for the Huai River dredging expenses, 20% for the Pearl River treatment expenses, 20% for the Yellow River treatment expenses, and the remaining 20% for construction projects under the Ministry of Industry. The main resolution passed at this Board of Directors meeting was to decide on the interest rate guarantee measures for the Boxer Indemnity so that the interest income is stable and can then be distributed to cultural and educational institutions. Therefore, from now on, all institutions borrowing funds must sign contracts in accordance with the interest rate guarantee measures and procedures resolved by the Board of Directors; otherwise, the funds cannot be paid. As for the 140,000 gold pounds in Huai River dredging expenses, it is the amount that the Huai River should receive and is not a special allocation. However, due to the severe floods and the urgency of the Huai River project, the Board of Directors will temporarily use it without having to pay it again in accordance with the interest rate guarantee measures. As for the flood relief case, the Chinese directors temporarily moved to request that some funds be allocated from the British Boxer Indemnity. After detailed discussions, it was determined that most of the British Boxer Indemnity is kept in the London Purchasing Committee, and the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Exchange of Notes was approved by the British Parliament and the uses have been designated. It would be difficult to change it now, so this case was not passed. The next meeting of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors is scheduled to be held in Beijing on November 4th.

Eurasian Aviation Corporation Convenes Shareholders Meeting

To Discuss Changing the Peiping-Manchouli Route

And Plans for the Northwest Route

The Eurasian Aviation Corporation has scheduled a shareholders meeting in Shanghai on the 28th of this month to discuss the development of the Northwest route and the reform of the Peiping-Manchouli route. The 8th Board of Directors meeting will be held on the same day to decide on the policy. Attendees at the Aviation East meeting include representatives from the Ministry of Transportation and representatives from the German Lufthansa Aviation Corporation. Attendees at the Board of Directors meeting include Chairman Wei Yifu, Vice Chairman Shuang Qing, Smidt, Director Liu Shufan, Li Jingcong, Lin Tianlan, Feng Yangke, Bolusen, etc. According to Sun Hegao, secretary of the Board of Directors, speaking to this newspaper's reporter yesterday, the Peiping-Manchouli route is now planned to be changed to Peiping to Taonan and then to Manchouli. The company sent aircraft and team leaders Smidt and Li Jingcong to inspect and test fly the route. Wireless equipment and various improvement equipment must be added along the way to ensure safety. After the two return, they will submit a report for the Board of Directors to review and handle. As for the two German pilots who were released from Outer Mongolia and returned to Peiping, the company has telegraphed them to rest in Peiping. The Northwest route is also being actively prepared. The route generally runs from Shanghai to Beijing, along the Longhai Line to Zhengzhou, then via Gansu, via Lanzhou and Dihua, and ends at Yili. It is more than twice as long as the Shanghai-Manchouli line, that is, about 5,000 miles long. Various plans will be discussed at this shareholders meeting and handed over to the Board of Directors for handling. It is expected that the route map will be surveyed and mapped and test flights will be prepared in a short period of time. New aircraft must also be purchased. After the Northwest route is opened, Eurasian mail can be smoothly delivered without being delayed by passing through Russia.

Peace Relief Issue

The Bankers' Association Discussed It Yesterday

The Result Was to First Telegraph Beiping to Inquire

The Shanghai Bankers' Association, for the purpose of promoting the issue of the Peace Relief Association, specially brought it up for discussion at yesterday morning's regular meeting. First, Mr. Lin Kanghou, a Standing Committee member of the Bankers' Association and initiator of the Relief Association, presented a telegram of support from Mr. Li Shizeng of Peiping, and a telegram from the Peace Relief Association initiated by all circles in Peiping a few days ago, advocating that in this autumn of major disasters, war should not be started again to cause misery to the people. All circles in the sea should jointly express their appeal for peace. However, empty words and indiscriminate telegrams may not help the facts. It is hoped that a good method can be found within the possible scope to seek salvation. The people present discussed it for a long time, and they all agreed that the desire for peace and disaster relief is shared by all Chinese people. However, the implementation plan must be carefully carried out in order to urge all parties to achieve effective results. As a result, it was resolved to first telegraph the Peiping Peace Relief Association to ask whether it has drafted a peace plan and to ask it to telegraph immediately so that all circles in the sea can proceed in an orderly manner and achieve the effect of unity between the north and the south.

Hu Lanqi Sails to Germany Today

After Mrs. Sun Soong Ching-ling came to Shanghai for the funeral, she rested in her Shanghai residence and declared that she had never heard of the peace movement.
